SENTIENT SPECIES:
Amorphous Robots with Five-fold Symmetry: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have five-fold symmetry and are able to greatly alter their shape. They are violent and unwilling to compromise. They were created by the Empire of Antoids and Robots on Taranis III as servants in 555.
	Their Stats are: STR: 2 DEX: 1 CON: 0 INT: 0 CHA: 1
Immortal Orange Antoids: Small, industrious and well-organised, these creatures' greatest weakness is their ever-ballooning population. They have orange skin. They have bilateral symmetry. They have no fixed lifespan and only die of disease or accidents. They are gregarious and have a complex system of social rules. They first evolved on Hylon VI in 302.
	Their Stats are: STR: -1 DEX: 0 CON: 0 INT: 0 CHA: 0
Telepathic Purple Robots with Threefold Symmetry: Purely mechanical lifeforms, artificially created. They have purple skin. They have trilateral symmetry. They can read each others' minds. They are humorless and strive to uphold their ideals of personal honour. They were created by the Republic of Antoids and Robots on Golet I as servants in 520.
	Their Stats are: STR: -2 DEX: 1 CON: 0 INT: 1 CHA: 0

CIVILISATIONS:
THE THIRD CHURCH OF SLIM ANTOIDS:
An ancient, corrupt, fantastically wealthy Church of 8 planets, with 24 billion inhabitants.
Major populations:
3 billion enslaved Amorphous Robots with Five-fold Symmetry.
13 billion enslaved Immortal Orange Antoids.
8 billion enslaved Telepathic Purple Robots with Threefold Symmetry.
It controls a Youth Serum.
It controls a Virtual Reality Matrix.
It is at war with the Empire of Immortal Orange Antoids.

	Their Stats are: STR: -7 DEX: -6 CON: -4 INT: -8 CHA: -6
THE EMPIRE OF IMMORTAL ORANGE ANTOIDS:
A young, fantastically wealthy Empire of 6 planets, with 12 billion inhabitants.
Major populations:
12 billion Immortal Orange Antoids.
It is at war with the Third Church of Slim Antoids.

	Their Stats are: STR: -7 DEX: -6 CON: -4 INT: -8 CHA: -6
